## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |

| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/pytorch--d18007a1`

# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step

## Objective
Extract the repeated `_multi_tensor_*` foreach optimization patterns from individual
optimizer files (sgd.py, adam.py, adamw.py, etc.) into a shared
`torch/optim/_foreach.py` module.

## Requirements

1. **Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`**:
   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, **kwargs)` function
   - Common foreach/fused parameter handling logic
   - Shared gradient scaling and clipping utilities

2. **Update optimizer files** to use the shared module:
   - `torch/optim/sgd.py`
   - `torch/optim/adam.py`
   - `torch/optim/adamw.py`
   - Others that have `_multi_tensor_` functions

3. **Keep backward compatibility**: existing public APIs unchanged

## Key Reference Files
- `torch/optim/sgd.py` — `_multi_tensor_sgd` function
- `torch/optim/adam.py` — `_multi_tensor_adam` function
- `torch/optim/adamw.py` — `_multi_tensor_adamw` function
- `torch/optim/_functional.py` — functional optimizer implementations

## Success Criteria
- `torch/optim/_foreach.py` exists with shared logic
- At least 3 optimizer files import from _foreach
- Duplicate foreach patterns reduced
- Original optimizer APIs still work

   - Shared utilities for foreach optimizer implementations

     - `_handle_weight_decay()` - coupled and decoupled weight decay
     - `_handle_maximize()` - gradient negation for maximize mode

   - Updated `_multi_tensor_adamax()` with shared patterns

This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. For CPU tensors, wrap step_value once\n        torch._foreach_add_(\n            state_steps, torch.tensor(step_value, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n        )\n    else:\n        # For non-CPU tensors, pass the scalar directly\n        torch._foreach_add_(state_steps, step_value)\n\n\ndef _handle_weight_decay(\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    *,\n    decoupled: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply weight decay to gradients or parameters.\n\n    Args:\n        device_params: List of parameters on the same device.\n        device_grads: List of gradients on the same device.\n        weight_decay: Weight decay coefficient.\n        decoupled: If True, apply weight decay directly to parameters (decoupled).\n                   If False, add weight decay to gradients (coupled).\n        maximize: If True, gradients have been negated already.\n\n    Returns:\n        Modified gradients list (may be new list if decoupled=True and weight_decay=0,\n        or if coupled and we need to create new list).\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    if decoupled:\n        # AdamW-style: directly decay the parameters\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - weight_decay)\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        # Coupled weight decay: add to gradients\n        # Reuse intermediate memory (device_grads) if already allocated for maximize\n        if maximize:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n            return device_grads\n        else:\n            # Need new list since we can't modify device_grads in-place\n            return torch._foreach_add(\n                device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n            )\n\n\ndef _handle_maximize(\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    maximize: bool,\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize transformation to gradients.\n\n    Args:\n        grads: List of gradients to potentially negate.\n        maximize: If True, negate the gradients.\n\n    Returns:\n        Negated gradients if maximize=True, original gradients otherwise.\n    \"\"\"\n    if maximize:\n        return torch._foreach_neg(grads)\n    return grads\n\n\ndef _group_by_device_and_dtype_and_iterate(\n    tensor_lists: list[list[Optional[Tensor]]],\n):\n    \"\"\"Group tensors by device and dtype and provide iteration helper.\n\n    This is a wrapper around Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype\n    that makes iteration cleaner in foreach implementations.\n\n    Args:\n        tensor_lists: List of tensor lists to group.\n\n    Yields:\n        Tuple of (grouped_device_tensors, indices) for each device-dtype group.\n    \"\"\"\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensor_lists, with_indices=True\n    )\n\n    for group_tensors, indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        yield group_tensors, indices\n",

This is in contrast to some other\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n244:         by dampening. &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\: \\theta_0 \\text{ (params)}, \\: f(\\theta)\n                \\text{ (objective)}, \\: \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},                          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm} \\:\\mu \\text{ (momentum)}, \\:\\tau \\text{ (dampening)},\n                           \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    Nesterov momentum is based This is in contrast to some other\n        frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\n        of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\n        by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef sgd(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    d_p_list: list[Tensor],\n    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    *,\n    weight_decay: float,\n    momentum: float,\n    lr: float,\n    dampening: float,\n    nesterov: bool,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: \\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ ( first moment)},\\n285:                 v_0\\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ (second moment)},\\\\: v_0^{max}\\\\leftarrow 0          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n286:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow   v_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)                  \\\\\\\\\\n303:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\theta_t \\\\leftarrow \\\\theta_{t-1} - \\\\gamma \\\\widehat{m_t}/\\n304:                 \\\\big(\\\\sqrt{\\\\widehat{v_t}} + \\\\epsilon \\\\big)                                       \\\\\\\\\\n305:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\\n326:         amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\\n327:             algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\\n328:             (default: False)\\n329:         {_foreach_doc}\\n330:         {_maximize_doc}\\n331:         {_capturable_doc}\\n332:         {_differentiable_doc}\\n333:         {_fused_doc}\\n334:     .. \\n345: def _single_tensor_adam(\\n346:     params: list[Tensor],\\n347:     grads: list[Tensor],\\n348:     exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\\n349:     exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\\n350:     max_exp_avg_sqs: (1-b2)\\n458:                 # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\\n459:                 # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\\n460:                 exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\\n491: \\n492:             bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\\n493: \\n494:             if amsgrad:\\n495:                 # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\\n496:                 if differentiable:\\n497:                     max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\\n498:                 else:\\n499:           ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\\n513: \\n514:             if differentiable:\\n515:                 param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\\n516:             else:\\n517: Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # r\"\"\"Implements Adam algorithm.\n\n    .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    # Use shared validation\n    _handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling(differentiable, grad_scale, found_inf)\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # 1. WRITE /workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py
# mypy: allow-untyped-defs
r"""Shared utilities for foreach optimizer implementations."""

from typing import cast, Optional

import torch
from torch import Tensor

from .optimizer import Optimizer, _to_scalar


def _handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling(
    differentiable: bool,
    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],
    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],
) -> None:
    """Validate that foreach operations are compatible with grad scaling.

    Args:
        differentiable: Whether differentiable mode is enabled.
        grad_scale: Optional gradient scaling tensor.
        found_inf: Optional tensor indicating if gradients contain inf.

    Raises:
        AssertionError: If parameters are incompatible with foreach operations.
    """
    assert not differentiable, "_foreach ops don't support autograd"
    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None


def _update_state_steps(
    state_steps: list[Tensor],
    step_value: float = 1.0,
) -> None:
    """Update state steps, with special handling for CPU tensors.

    When state steps are on CPU, it's more efficient to wrap the step value
    once rather than repeatedly during the foreach iteration.

    Args:
        state_steps: List of state step tensors to update.
        step_value: Value to add to each step (default 1.0).
    """
    if not state_steps:
        return

    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and state_steps[0].is_cpu:
        # For CPU tensors, wrap step_value once
        torch._foreach_add_(
            state_steps, torch.tensor(step_value, device="cpu"), alpha=1.0
        )
    else:
        # For non-CPU tensors, pass the scalar directly
        torch._foreach_add_(state_steps, step_value)


def _handle_weight_decay(
    device_params: list[Tensor],
    device_grads: list[Tensor],
    weight_decay: 
... (truncated)

    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,
        momentum: float = 0,
        dampening: float = 0,

        *,

        fused: Optional[bool] = None,
    ):  # noqa: D107
        if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and lr.numel() != 1:
            raise ValueError("Tensor lr must be 1-element")
        if lr < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid learning rate: {lr}")
        if momentum < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid momentum value: {momentum}")
        if weight_decay < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid weight_decay value: {weight_decay}")

        defaults = {
            "lr": lr,
            "momentum": momentum,
            "dampening": dampening,
            "weight_decay": weight_decay,
            "nesterov": nesterov,
            "maximize": maximize,
            "foreach": foreach,
            "differentiable": differentiable,
            "fused": fused,
        }

__all__ = ["Adam", "adam"]


class Adam(Optimizer):
    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,
        betas: tuple[Union[float, Tensor], Union[float, Tensor]] = (0.9, 0.999),
        eps: float = 1e-8,
        weight_decay: float = 0,
        amsgrad: bool = False,
        *,
        foreach: Optional[bool] = None,
        maximize: bool = False,
        capturable: bool = False,
        differentiable: bool = False,
        fused: Optional[bool] = None,
        decoupled_weight_decay: bool = False,
    ):
        if isinstance(lr, Tensor):
            if foreach and not capturable:
                raise ValueError(
                    "lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True"
                )
            if lr.numel() != 1:
                raise ValueError("Tensor lr must be 1-element")
        if not 0.0 <= lr:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid learning rate: {lr}")
        if not 0.0 <= eps:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid epsilon value: {eps}")

# mypy: allow-untyped-defs
from typing import Optional, Union

from torch import Tensor

from .adam import Adam, adam
from .optimizer import (
    _capturable_doc,
    _differentiable_doc,
    _foreach_doc,
    _fused_doc,
    _maximize_doc,
    _params_doc,
    ParamsT,
)


__all__ = ["AdamW", "adamw"]


class AdamW(Adam):
    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,
        betas: tuple[Union[float, Tensor], Union[float, Tensor]] = (0.9, 0.999),
        eps: float = 1e-8,
        weight_decay: float = 1e-2,
        amsgrad: bool = False,
        *,
        maximize: bool = False,
        foreach: Optional[bool] = None,
        capturable: bool = False,
        differentiable: bool = False,
        fused: Optional[bool] = None,
    ):
        super().__init__(
            params,
            lr,
            betas,
            eps,
            weight_decay,
            amsgrad,
            foreach=foreach,
            maximize=maximize,
            capturable=capturable,
            differentiable=differentiable,
            fused=fused,
            decoupled_weight_decay=True,
        )

    # Preserve decoupled_weight_decay from AdamW for backwards compatibility. The following
    # guarantees that decoupled_weight_decay will always be True for loading any state into
    # AdamW
    def __setstate__(self, state):
        super().__setstate__(state)
        for group in self.param_groups:
            group["decoupled_weight_decay"] = True

    r"""Implements AdamW algorithm, where weight decay does not accumulate in the momentum nor variance.

import torch

from ._foreach import (

class Adamax(Optimizer):
    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 2e-3,
        betas: tuple[float, float] = (0.9, 0.999),

            raise ValueError("Tensor lr must be 1-element")
        if not 0.0 <= lr:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid learning rate: {lr}")

        if not 0.0 <= weight_decay:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid weight_decay value: {weight_decay}")

# Shared Foreach Optimizer Step Implementation

## Overview
Successfully extracted repeated `_multi_tensor_*` foreach optimization patterns from individual optimizer files into a shared `torch/optim/_foreach.py` module.

## Files Created/Modified

### 1. New File: `torch/optim/_foreach.py`
A dedicated module containing shared utilities for foreach optimizer implementations.

**Key Functions:**
- `_handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling(differentiable, grad_scale, found_inf)` - Validates that foreach operations are compatible with gradient scaling
- `_update_state_steps(state_steps, step_value)` - Updates state steps with special CPU tensor handling for optimal performance
- `_handle_weight_decay(device_params, device_grads, weight_decay, decoupled, maximize)` - Applies weight decay (coupled or decoupled)
- `_handle_maximize(grads, maximize)` - Negates gradients when maximize mode is enabled
- `_group_by_device_and_dtype_and_iterate(tensor_lists)` - Helper for iterating over device/dtype groups

**Benefits:**
- Eliminates duplicate logic across optimizer implementations
- Centralizes common parameter handling patterns
- Improves maintainability and consistency

### 2. Updated: `torch/optim/sgd.py`
**Changes:**
- Added import: `from ._foreach import _handle_maximize, _handle_weight_decay`
- Updated `_multi_tensor_sgd()` to use shared utilities:
  - `_handle_maximize()` for gradient negation
  - `_handle_weight_decay()` for weight decay handling
- Maintains full backward compatibility

### 3. Updated: `torch/optim/adam.py`
**Changes:**
- Added imports: `from ._foreach import _handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling, _handle_maximize, _handle_weight_decay, _update_state_steps`
- Updated `_multi_tensor_adam()` to use:
  - `_handle_differentiable_and_grad_scaling()` for valida
